                <a class="m-card--header" href="/trawler-news/soundings-drowning-doesnt-look-like-drowning" phx-track-event="" phx-track-id="Title" rel="nofollow">
                 <h2 class="m-card--header-text" phx-ellipsis="" role="heading">
                  Drowning Doesn't Look Like Drowning
                 </h2>
                </a>
                <p class="m-card--body" phx-ellipsis="">
                 Mention drowning and we all tend to envision a person in the water waving his hands, splashing and screaming for help. Thats not even remotely close to what a drowning person looks like, writes Mario Vittone in this weeks Lifelines: Safety And Rescue At Sea blog.
                </p>
               </div>
              </article>
